   &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;(837&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Net operating loss carry-forward and credits&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;77&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;96&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: white&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Valuation allowance established against state NOL&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;(77&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;-&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt; padding-left: 20pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Non-current tax assets, net&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;$&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;10,040&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;$&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;14,532&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Accounting Standards Codification&#13;(&amp;#8220;ASC&amp;#8221;) 740 requires that an entity&amp;#8217;s deferred tax assets be reduced by a valuation allowance to the extent its&#13;management determines that it is more likely than not that such deferred tax asset, or portion thereof, will not be realized. Management&#13;evaluated the realizability of its deferred tax assets to determine the need and appropriateness of a valuation allowance. In its&#13;determinations, Management considers items of evidence, both positive and negative, including those items outlined in ASC 740.&#13;The Company policy outlines measurable objective criteria that must be met before a release of the valuation allowance will occur.&#13;The three criteria set forth in the policy must all be satisfied before the valuation allowance can be reversed. The three criteria&#13;were met and the valuation allowance was reversed in its entirety during fiscal year 2015. The Company continues to measure the&#13;realizability of its deferred tax assets against the preset criteria. The criteria are as follows: first, the Company&amp;#8217;s available&#13;federal tax net operating loss (&amp;#8220;NOL&amp;#8221;) must be zero; second, the prior thirty-six month cumulative book basis pre-tax&#13;income (loss), after considering &amp;#8220;one-time&amp;#8221; events, is positive; third, the Company considers its outlook of near term&#13;continued profitable operations and assesses any material negative and positive trends or events on the immediate horizon. As of&#13;November 3, 2017, the Company (1) has utilized its entire federal net operating loss, (2) has positive thirty-six month cumulative&#13;book income and (3) positive economic factors including more stable commodity markets and current profitable operations are present.&#13;Management reevaluated the need for a full valuation allowance as of November 3, 2017 and determined that some of its California&#13;NOL may not be utilized. Therefore a valuation allowance of $77 has been provided for such portion of California NOL.&amp;#160; Management&#13;has concluded that it is more likely than not that the other deferred tax assets as of November 3, 2017 will be realized.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Due to the degree of judgment&#13;involved, actual taxable income could differ materially from management&amp;#8217;s estimates, or the timing of taxable income could&#13;be such that the net operating losses could expire prior to their utilization. Management could determine in the future that the&#13;assets are unrealizable, materially decreasing net income in one or more periods. Following recognition, management could reinstate&#13;a full valuation allowance should operating performance decline.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;As of November 3, 2017&#13;the Company had net operating loss carryforwards of approximately $874 for state purposes.&amp;#160; These loss carryforwards will&#13;expire at various dates from 2022 through 2033.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In July 2006, the FASB&#13;issued guidance to clarify the accounting for uncertainty in income taxes recognized in an enterprise&amp;#8217;s financial statements.&#13;This interpretation prescribed a recognition threshold and measurement attribute for the financial statement recognition and measurement&#13;of a tax position taken or expected to be taken in a tax return. The guidance also discussed derecognition, classification, interest&#13;and penalties, accounting in interim periods, disclosure, and transition. The provisions of this guidance have been incorporated&#13;into ASC 740-10.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In November 2015, the&#13;FASB issued guidance in ASU 2015-17 concerning the balance sheet classification of deferred taxes in an initiative to reduce complexity&#13;in accounting standards. All deferred tax liabilities and assets should now be classified as noncurrent in the statement of financial&#13;position to simplify presentation of deferred tax assets. The guidance is effective for financial statements issued for annual&#13;periods beginning after December 15, 2016. We have already adopted this guidance and the change is reflected as of October 28,&#13;2016.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;As of November 3, 2017,&#13;we have provided a liability of $135 for unrecognized tax benefits related to various federal and state income tax matters. A significant&#13;portion of this amount would generally reduce our effective income tax rate if recognized in future reporting periods. We have&#13;not identified any new unrecognized tax benefits.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;As of October 28, 2016,&#13;we have provided a liability of $130 for unrecognized tax benefits related to various federal and state income tax matters. A significant&#13;portion of this amount would generally reduce our effective income tax rate if recognized in future reporting periods. We have&#13;not identified any new unrecognized tax benefits.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 3 - &lt;i&gt;Retirement and Other Benefit Plans:&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Noncontributory-Trusteed&#13;Defined Benefit Retirement Plans for Sales, Administrative, Supervisory and Certain Other Employees&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We have noncontributory-trusteed&#13;defined benefit retirement plans for sales, administrative, supervisory and certain other employees. In the third quarter of fiscal&#13;year 2006, we froze future benefit accruals under this plan for employees classified within the administrative, sales or supervisory&#13;job classifications or within any non-bargaining class. The benefits under these plans are primarily based on years of service&#13;and compensation levels. The funding policy of the plan requires contributions which are at least equal to the minimum required&#13;contributions needed to avoid a funding deficiency. The measurement date for the plan is our fiscal year end.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We perform an internal&#13;rate of return analysis when making the discount rate selection. The discount rates were based on Citigroup Pension Liability Index&#13;as of October 31, 2017 and September 30, 2016, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Plan assets are primarily&#13;invested in marketable equity securities, corporate and government debt securities and are administered by an investment management&#13;company. The plans&amp;#8217; long-term return on assets is based on the weighted-average of the plans&amp;#8217; investment allocation&#13;as of the measurement date and the published historical returns for those types of asset categories, taking into consideration&#13;inflation rate forecasts. Our expected employer contribution to the plan in fiscal year 2018 is $1,150.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;During fiscal year 2015,&#13;our actuary updated mortality tables from the IRS 2014 Combined Static Mortality assumptions to the SOA RP 2014 Total Dataset Adjusted&#13;to 2006 with Scale MP-2015. The change in mortality table resulted in a significant liability increase in fiscal year 2015 as well&#13;as an increased net periodic pension cost (NPPC) projection for fiscal year 2016. The expected rate of return on plan assets remained&#13;the same at 7.00% effective for fiscal years 2017 and 2016, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Executive Retirement Plans&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Non-Qualified Deferred Compensation&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Effective January 1, 1991,&#13;we adopted a deferred compensation savings plan for certain key employees. Under this arrangement, selected employees contribute&#13;a portion of their annual compensation to the plan. We contribute an amount to each participant&amp;#8217;s account by computing an&#13;investment return equal to Moody&amp;#8217;s Average Seasoned Bond Rate plus 2%. Employees receive vested amounts upon death, termination&#13;or attainment of retirement age. No benefit expense was recorded under these plans for fiscal years 2017 and 2016.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Supplemental Executive Retirement Plan&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In fiscal year 1991, we&#13;adopted a non-qualified supplemental retirement plan for certain key employees. Benefits provided under the plan are equal to 60%&#13;of the employee&amp;#8217;s final average earnings, less amounts provided by our defined benefit pension plan and amounts available&#13;through Social Security.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Benefits payable related&#13;to these plans and included in the accompanying consolidated financial statements were $5,607 and $5,454 as of November 3, 2017&#13;and October 28, 2016, respectively. In connection with these arrangements we are the beneficiary of life insurance policies on&#13;the lives of certain key employees and retirees. The aggregate cash surrender value of these policies, included in non-current&#13;assets, was $13,105 and $13,769 as of November 3, 2017 and October 28, 2016, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We provide an incentive&#13;compensation plan for certain key executives, which is based upon our pretax income. The payment of these amounts is generally&#13;deferred over three or five-year periods. The total amount payable related to this arrangement was $10,530 and $7,098 as of November&#13;3, 2017 and October 28, 2016, respectively. Future payments are approximately $4,502, $3,745, $2,089, $132 and $63 for fiscal years&#13;2018 through 2022, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Use of estimates and assumptions&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;The preparation of financial&#13;statements in conformity with generally accepted accounting principles requires management to make certain estimates and assumptions&#13;that affect the reported amounts of assets and liabilities and disclosure of contingent assets and liabilities at the date of the&#13;financial statements, as well as the reported revenues and expenses during the respective reporting periods. Actual results could&#13;differ from those estimates. Amounts estimated related to liabilities for pension benefits, self-insured workers&amp;#8217; compensation&#13;and employee healthcare benefits are subject to inherent uncertainties and these estimated liabilities may ultimately settle at&#13;amounts which may vary from current estimates. Other areas with underlying estimates include realization of deferred tax assets,&#13;cash surrender or contract value of life insurance policies, promotional allowances and the allowance for doubtful accounts and&#13;inventory reserves. Management believes its current estimates are reasonable and based on the best information available at the&#13;time.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Concentrations of credit risk&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Our credit risk is diversified&#13;across a broad range of customers and geographic regions. Losses due to credit risk have recently been immaterial. The carrying&#13;amount of cash equivalents, accounts and other receivables, accounts payable and accrued liabilities approximate fair market value&#13;due to the short maturity of these instruments. We maintain cash balances at financial institutions, which may at times exceed&#13;the amounts insured by the Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation. Management does not believe there is significant credit risk&#13;associated with these financial institutions. The provision for doubtful accounts receivable is based on historical trends and&#13;current collectability risk.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Revenues&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Revenues are recognized&#13;upon passage of title to the customer, typically upon product pick-up, shipment or delivery to customers. Products are delivered&#13;to customers primarily through our own long-haul fleet or through a Company owned direct store delivery system. These delivery&#13;costs, $3,556 and $3,456 for fiscal years 2017 and 2016, respectively, are included in selling, general and administrative expenses&#13;in the accompanying consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Cash and cash equivalents&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Fair value measurements&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We classify levels of inputs to measure the&#13;fair value of financial assets as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 24px&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 1 inputs: Level 1 inputs are quoted market prices in active markets for identical assets or liabilities that are accessible at the measurement date. &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 2 inputs: Level 2 inputs are from other than quoted market prices included in Level 1 that are observable for the asset or liability, either directly or indirectly.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 3 inputs: Level 3 inputs are unobservable and should be used to measure fair value to the extent that observable inputs are not available.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;The hierarchy noted above&#13;requires us to minimize the use of unobservable inputs and to use observable market data, if available, when determining fair value.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Inventories&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Property, plant and equipment&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Capital leases&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Life insurance policies&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Income taxes&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Deferred taxes are provided&#13;for items whose financial and tax bases differ. A valuation allowance is provided against deferred tax assets when it is expected&#13;that it is more likely than not that the related asset will not be fully realized. The determination as to whether or not a deferred&#13;tax asset can be fully realized is subject to a significant degree of judgment, based at least partially upon a projection of future&#13;taxable income, which takes into consideration past and future trends in profitability, customer demand, supply costs, and multiple&#13;other factors, none of which are predictable.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Times

 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Comprehensive income&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Recently issued accounting pronouncements&#13;and regulations&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In May 2014, the Financial&#13;Accounting Standards Board (the &amp;#8220;FASB&amp;#8221;) issued ASU 2014-09 &amp;#8220;Revenue from Contracts with Customers&amp;#8221; to supersede&#13;previous revenue recognition guidance under current U.S. GAAP. The guidance presents a single five-step model for comprehensive&#13;revenue recognition that requires an entity to recognize revenue to depict the transfer of promised goods or services to customers&#13;in an amount that reflects the consideration to which the entity expects to be entitled in exchange for those goods or services.&#13;Two options are available for implementation of the standard which are either the retrospective approach or cumulative effect adjustment&#13;approach. The guidance becomes effective for annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2017, including interim periods&#13;within that reporting period, with early adoption permitted. The Company anticipates using the modified retrospective transition&#13;method beginning with the first quarter of fiscal 2019. The Company is in the process of evaluating the full impact of adoption&#13;of this guidance and does not presently expect adoption to have a material impact on its consolidated financial statements aside&#13;from more detailed and improved disclosure requirements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In July 2015, the FASB&#13;issued ASU 2015-11 &amp;#8220;Simplifying the Measurement of Inventory&amp;#8221;. The guidance is part of the &amp;#8220;Simplification Initiative&amp;#8221;&#13;to identify and re-evaluate areas where the generally accepted accounting principles may be complex and cumbersome to apply. The&#13;guidance will require that inventory be stated at the lower of cost and net realizable value as opposed to the lower of cost or&#13;market. Net realizable value is the estimated selling price for the inventory less completion, disposal and transportation costs.&#13;The guidance became effective for fiscal years beginning after December 15, 2016. The Company already values inventory by the proposed&#13;method.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In November 2015, the&#13;FASB issued ASU 2015-17, &amp;#8220;Balance Sheet Classification of Deferred Taxes&amp;#8221;. The guidance requires that all deferred&#13;tax assets and liabilities, along with any related valuation allowance, be classified as noncurrent on the balance sheet. The guidance&#13;becomes effective for annual reporting periods beginning after December 6, 2016 with early adoption permitted. The Company applied&#13;this guidance to its fiscal year ended November 3, 2017. Adoption of this guidance had no material impact on the results of operations&#13;or financial position.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In February 2016, the&#13;FASB issued ASU 2016-02, &amp;#8220;Leases&amp;#8221;. The guidance requires both operating and capital leases to be recognized on the&#13;balance sheet. The guidance becomes effective for annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2018 with early adoption&#13;permitted. The adoption of this guidance is not expected to have a material impact on the Company&amp;#8217;s consolidated financial&#13;statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In October 2016, the FASB&#13;issued ASU 2016-16, &amp;#8220;Income Taxes &amp;#8211; Classification of Certain Cash Receipts and Cash Payments&amp;#8221;. The guidance&#13;involves eight specific cash flow issues and aims to unify accounting for these transactions. The guidance becomes effective for&#13;annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2017 with early adoption permitted. The Company is currently evaluating this&#13;guidance and its impact on its results of operations or financial position.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

   &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt; text-align: right&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt; text-align: right&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;(a) Minimum payments exclude contingent rentals&#13;based on actual mileage and adjustments of rental payments based on the Consumer Price Index. Contingent rentals amounted to $56&#13;in fiscal year 2017 and $66 in fiscal year 2016 including prior lease arrangements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;(b) Amount necessary to reduce net minimum&#13;lease payments to present value calculated at our incremental borrowing rate at the inception of the leases.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 1 - &lt;i&gt;The Company and Summary of Significant Accounting&#13;Policies:&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Bridgford Foods Corporation&#13;was organized in 1952. We originally began operations in 1932 as a retail meat market in San Diego, California and evolved into&#13;a meat wholesaler for hotels and restaurants, a distributor of frozen food products, a processor and packer of meat, and a manufacturer&#13;and distributor of frozen food products for sale on a retail and wholesale basis. For more than the past five years we and our&#13;subsidiaries have been primarily engaged in the manufacturing, marketing and distribution of an extensive line of frozen, refrigerated,&#13;and snack food products throughout the United States.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;The consolidated financial&#13;statements include the accounts of the Company and its subsidiaries, all of which are wholly-owned. All inter-company transactions&#13;have been eliminated.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Use of estimates and assumptions&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;The preparation of financial&#13;statements in conformity with generally accepted accounting principles requires management to make certain estimates and assumptions&#13;that affect the reported amounts of assets and liabilities and disclosure of contingent assets and liabilities at the date of the&#13;financial statements, as well as the reported revenues and expenses during the respective reporting periods. Actual results could&#13;differ from those estimates. Amounts estimated related to liabilities for pension benefits, self-insured workers&amp;#8217; compensation&#13;and employee healthcare benefits are subject to inherent uncertainties and these estimated liabilities may ultimately settle at&#13;amounts which may vary from current estimates. Other areas with underlying estimates include realization of deferred tax assets,&#13;cash surrender or contract value of life insurance policies, promotional allowances and the allowance for doubtful accounts and&#13;inventory reserves. Management believes its current estimates are reasonable and based on the best information available at the&#13;time.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;We test long-lived assets&#13;for recoverability whenever events or changes in circumstances indicate that the carrying amount may not be recoverable. If an&#13;impairment is indicated, we measure the fair value of assets to determine if and when adjustments are recorded.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Subsequent events&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Management has evaluated&#13;events subsequent to November 3, 2017 through the date the accompanying consolidated financial statements were filed with the Securities&#13;and Exchange Commission for transactions and other events that may require adjustment of and/or disclosure in such financial statements.&#13;On December 22, 2017, the President of the United States signed into law the Tax Cuts and Jobs Act which reforms U.S. Tax legislation&#13;and related laws. One of the provisions of the new tax law reduces the company&amp;#8217;s U.S. federal corporate income tax rate from&#13;the current 34% to 21%. This legislation was enacted after the close of our 2017 fiscal year end. The Company&amp;#8217;s effective&#13;tax rate for the fifty-three weeks ended November 3, 2017 does not include the impact of the Tax Cut and Jobs Act. Our deferred&#13;tax assets will be revalued at the lower rate during the first quarter of fiscal 2018 ending January 26, 2018. The Company continues&#13;to evaluate the impact of the new tax law on its financial condition and results of operations. Based on management&amp;#8217;s review,&#13;no other material events were identified that require adjustment to the financial statements or additional disclosure.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Concentrations of credit risk&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Our credit risk is diversified&#13;across a broad range of customers and geographic regions. Losses due to credit risk have recently been immaterial. The carrying&#13;amount of cash equivalents, accounts and other receivables, accounts payable and accrued liabilities approximate fair market value&#13;due to the short maturity of these instruments. We maintain cash balances at financial institutions, which may at times exceed&#13;the amounts insured by the Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation. Management does not believe there is significant credit risk&#13;associated with these financial institutions. The provision for doubtful accounts receivable is based on historical trends and&#13;current collectability risk.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;We have significant accounts&#13;receivable with a few large, well known customers which, although historically secure, could be subject to material risk should&#13;these customers&amp;#8217; operations suddenly deteriorate. Sales to Wal-Mart&amp;#174; comprised 37.7% of revenues in fiscal 2017 and&#13;36.9% of total accounts receivable was due from Wal-Mart&amp;#174; as of November 3, 2017. Sales to Wal-Mart&amp;#174; comprised 34.8%&#13;of revenues in fiscal 2016 and 35.6% of total accounts receivable was due from Wal-Mart as of &amp;#174; October 28, 2016.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Business segments&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Our company and its subsidiaries&#13;operate in two business segments - the processing and distribution of frozen foods products, and the processing and distribution&#13;of snack food products. See Note 7 to the Consolidated Financial Statements for further information.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Fiscal year&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;We maintain our accounting&#13;records on a 52-53 week fiscal basis ending on the Friday closest to October 31. As part of the regular accounting cycle, fiscal&#13;year 2017 included 53 weeks and fiscal year 2016 included 52 weeks.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 7.5pt; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Revenues&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Revenues are recognized&#13;upon passage of title to the customer, typically upon product pick-up, shipment or delivery to customers. Products are delivered&#13;to customers primarily through our own long-haul fleet or through a Company owned direct store delivery system. These delivery&#13;costs, $3,556 and $3,456 for fiscal years 2017 and 2016, respectively, are included in selling, general and administrative expenses&#13;in the accompanying consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We record promotional&#13;and returns allowances based on recent and historical trends. Revenue is recognized as the net amount estimated to be received&#13;after deducting estimated amounts for discounts, trade allowances and product returns. Promotional allowances, including customer&#13;incentive and trade promotion activities, are recorded as a reduction to sales based on amounts estimated being due to customers,&#13;based primarily on historical utilization and redemption rates. Promotional allowances deducted from sales for fiscal years 2017&#13;and 2016 were $9,123 and $8,578, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Advertising expenses&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Advertising and other&#13;promotional expenses are recorded as selling, general and administrative expenses. Advertising expenses for fiscal years 2017 and&#13;2016 were $2,403 and $2,055, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Cash and cash equivalents&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We consider all investments&#13;with original maturities of three months or less to be cash equivalents. Cash equivalents include money market funds and treasury&#13;bills. Cash equivalents totaled $12,109 as of November 3, 2017 and $6,985 as of October 28, 2016. All material cash and cash equivalents&#13;as of November 3, 2017 were held at Wells Fargo Bank N.A.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Fair value measurements&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We classify levels of inputs to measure the&#13;fair value of financial assets as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 24px&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 1 inputs: Level 1 inputs are quoted market prices in active markets for identical assets or liabilities that are accessible at the measurement date. &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 2 inputs: Level 2 inputs are from other than quoted market prices included in Level 1 that are observable for the asset or liability, either directly or indirectly.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 3 inputs: Level 3 inputs are unobservable and should be used to measure fair value to the extent that observable inputs are not available.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;The hierarchy noted above&#13;requires us to minimize the use of unobservable inputs and to use observable market data, if available, when determining fair value.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;The Company does not have&#13;any assets or liabilities measured at fair value on a recurring or non-recurring basis for the fiscal years ended November 3, 2017&#13;and October 28, 2016.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Inventories&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Inventories are valued&#13;at the lower of cost (which approximates actual cost on a first-in, first-out basis) or market. Costs related to warehousing, transportation&#13;and distribution to customers are considered when computing market value. Inventories include the cost of raw materials, labor&#13;and manufacturing overhead. We regularly review inventory quantities on hand and write down any excess or obsolete inventories&#13;to net realizable value. An inventory reserve is created when potentially slow-moving or obsolete inventories are identified in&#13;order to reflect the appropriate inventory value. Changes in economic conditions, production requirements, and lower than expected&#13;customer demand could result in additional obsolete or slow-moving inventory that cannot be sold or must be sold at reduced prices&#13;and could result in additional reserve provisions.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Property, plant and equipment&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Property, plant and equipment&#13;are carried at cost less accumulated depreciation. Major renewals and improvements are charged to the asset accounts while the&#13;cost of maintenance and repairs is charged to expense as incurred. When assets are sold or otherwise disposed of, the cost and&#13;accumulated depreciation are removed from the respective accounts and the resulting gain or loss is credited or charged to income.&#13;Depreciation is computed on a straight-line basis over 10 to 20 years for buildings and improvements, 5 to 10 years for machinery&#13;and equipment, and 3 to 5 years for transportation equipment.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Capital leases&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Leased property and equipment&#13;that meet capital lease criteria are capitalized at the lower of the present value of the minimum payments required under the lease&#13;or the fair value of the asset at inception of the lease and are included within property, plant and equipment on the consolidated&#13;balance sheet. Obligations under capital leases are accounted for as current and noncurrent liabilities on the consolidated balance&#13;sheet. Amortization is calculated on a straight-line method based upon the shorter of the estimated useful life of the asset or&#13;the lease term.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Life insurance policies&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;We record the cash surrender&#13;value or contract value for life insurance policies as an adjustment of premiums paid in determining the expense or income to be&#13;recognized under the contract for the period. The cash surrender value is included in other non-current assets in the accompanying&#13;consolidated balance sheets.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Income taxes&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27pt&gt;Deferred taxes are provided&#13;for items whose financial and tax bases differ. A valuation allowance is provided against deferred tax assets when it is expected&#13;that it is more likely than not that the related asset will not be fully realized. The determination as to whether or not a deferred&#13;tax asset can be fully realized is subject to a significant degree of judgment, based at least partially upon a projection of future&#13;taxable income, which takes into consideration past and future trends in profitability, customer demand, supply costs, and multiple&#13;other factors, none of which are predictable.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We provide tax accruals&#13;for federal, state and local exposures relating to audit results, tax planning initiatives and compliance responsibilities. The&#13;development of these accruals requires judgments about tax issues, potential outcomes and timing. (See Note 4 to the Consolidated&#13;Financial Statements). Although the outcome of these tax audits is uncertain, in management&amp;#8217;s opinion adequate provisions&#13;for income taxes have been made for potential liabilities emanating from these reviews. If actual outcomes differ materially from&#13;these estimates, they could have a material impact on our results of operations.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Stock-based compensation&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;We measure and recognize&#13;compensation expense for all share-based payments to employees, including grants of employee stock options, in the financial statements&#13;based on the fair value at the date of the grant. We have not issued, awarded, granted or entered into any stock-based payment&#13;agreements since April 29, 1999.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Comprehensive income&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;Comprehensive income consists of net income&#13;and additional minimum pension liability adjustments.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Recently issued accounting pronouncements&#13;and regulations&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In May 2014, the Financial&#13;Accounting Standards Board (the &amp;#8220;FASB&amp;#8221;) issued ASU 2014-09 &amp;#8220;Revenue from Contracts with Customers&amp;#8221; to supersede&#13;previous revenue recognition guidance under current U.S. GAAP. The guidance presents a single five-step model for comprehensive&#13;revenue recognition that requires an entity to recognize revenue to depict the transfer of promised goods or services to customers&#13;in an amount that reflects the consideration to which the entity expects to be entitled in exchange for those goods or services.&#13;Two options are available for implementation of the standard which are either the retrospective approach or cumulative effect adjustment&#13;approach. The guidance becomes effective for annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2017, including interim periods&#13;within that reporting period, with early adoption permitted. The Company anticipates using the modified retrospective transition&#13;method beginning with the first quarter of fiscal 2019. The Company is in the process of evaluating the full impact of adoption&#13;of this guidance and does not presently expect adoption to have a material impact on its consolidated financial statements aside&#13;from more detailed and improved disclosure requirements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In July 2015, the FASB&#13;issued ASU 2015-11 &amp;#8220;Simplifying the Measurement of Inventory&amp;#8221;. The guidance is part of the &amp;#8220;Simplification Initiative&amp;#8221;&#13;to identify and re-evaluate areas where the generally accepted accounting principles may be complex and cumbersome to apply. The&#13;guidance will require that inventory be stated at the lower of cost and net realizable value as opposed to the lower of cost or&#13;market. Net realizable value is the estimated selling price for the inventory less completion, disposal and transportation costs.&#13;The guidance became effective for fiscal years beginning after December 15, 2016. The Company already values inventory by the proposed&#13;method.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In November 2015, the&#13;FASB issued ASU 2015-17, &amp;#8220;Balance Sheet Classification of Deferred Taxes&amp;#8221;. The guidance requires that all deferred&#13;tax assets and liabilities, along with any related valuation allowance, be classified as noncurrent on the balance sheet. The guidance&#13;becomes effective for annual reporting periods beginning after December 6, 2016 with early adoption permitted. The Company applied&#13;this guidance to its fiscal year ended November 3, 2017. Adoption of this guidance had no material impact on the results of operations&#13;or financial position.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In February 2016, the&#13;FASB issued ASU 2016-02, &amp;#8220;Leases&amp;#8221;. The guidance requires both operating and capital leases to be recognized on the&#13;balance sheet. The guidance becomes effective for annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2018 with early adoption&#13;permitted. The adoption of this guidance is not expected to have a material impact on the Company&amp;#8217;s consolidated financial&#13;statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.35in&gt;In October 2016, the FASB&#13;issued ASU 2016-16, &amp;#8220;Income Taxes &amp;#8211; Classification of Certain Cash Receipts and Cash Payments&amp;#8221;. The guidance&#13;involves eight specific cash flow issues and aims to unify accounting for these transactions. The guidance becomes effective for&#13;annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2017 with early adoption permitted. The Company is currently evaluating this&#13;guidance and its impact on its results of operations or financial position.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

var Show = {};
Show.LastAR = null
Show.hideAR = function(){
	Show.LastAR.style.display = 'none';
};
Show.showAR = function ( link
 id
 win ){
	if( Show.LastAR ){
		Show.hideAR();
	}
	var ref = link;
	do {
		ref = ref.nextSibling;
	} while (ref && ref.nodeName != 'TABLE');
	if (!ref || ref.nodeName != 'TABLE') {
		var tmp = win ?
			win.document.getElementById(id) :
			document.getElementById(id);
		if( tmp ){
			ref = tmp.cloneNode(true);
			ref.id = '';
			link.parentNode.appendChild(ref);
		}
	}
	if( ref ){
		ref.style.display = 'block';
		Show.LastAR = ref;
	}
};
Show.toggleNext = function( link ){
	var ref = link;
	do{
		ref = ref.nextSibling;
	}while( ref.nodeName != 'DIV' );
	if( ref.style &&
		ref.style.display &&
		ref.style.display == 'none' ){
		ref.style.display = 'block';
		if( link.textContent ){
			link.textContent = link.textContent.replace( '+'
 '-' );
		}else{
			link.innerText = link.innerText.replace( '+'
 '-' );
		}
	}else{
		ref.style.display = 'none';
		if( link.textContent ){
			link.textContent = link.textContent.replace( '-'
 '+' );
		}else{
			link.innerText = link.innerText.replace( '-'
 '+' );
		}
	}
};
